<script type="text/javascript">
    /**
     *  key: 模块名称，可以使用VersionHub.get()方法获取相应模块的命中规则的放量版本名称
     *  version: 版本名称
     *  percent: 放量比例
     *  forceMid： 是否使用mid
     *  offline: 是否下线
     *  custom: 使用自定义条件
     */
    VersionHub.resolve({
        searchInput: [
            {
                version: 'search_input_ver_a',
                percent: [15, 25]
            },
            {
                version: 'search_input_ver_b',
                percent: [25, 35]
            }
        ],
        famousSiteRec: [
            {
                version: 'fsReplace',
                percent: [35, 36],
                custom: function () {
                    var seedSign = parseInt((UserTool.getCookieSeed('__guid')
                        || UserTool.getCookieSeed('sessionID')
                        || Math.random() * 100000) / 1000);
                    return (seedSign == 7 || seedSign == 8) && hao360.cityCode.get() != "101010100";
                }
            },
            {
                version: 'fsReplaceCompare',
                percent: [35, 36],
                custom: function () {
                    var seedSign = parseInt((UserTool.getCookieSeed('__guid')
                        || UserTool.getCookieSeed('sessionID')
                        || Math.random() * 100000) / 1000);
                    return (seedSign == 5 || seedSign == 6) && hao360.cityCode.get() != "101010100";
                }
            },
            {

                (function(){
                    var config = HAO_CONFIG.search,
                        searchData = new AppData('api.hao.360.cn', config.r),
                        defaultEng = searchData.get('defaultEng')||"somulti",
                        g = hao360.g;
                    if(/^\?1009(\W|$)/.test(location.search)){
                        defaultEng = 'so360';
                        hao360.g('search-engine').className = 'single';
                    }

                    (function () {
                        var COOKIE_KEY = 'somultiswitch';
                        var cookieVal = qboot.cookie.get(COOKIE_KEY);

                        if (cookieVal === '1') {
                            LogHub.behavior('somultiswitch', 'soeng' + cookieVal);
                            return;
                        }

                        if (defaultEng === 'somulti') {
                            cookieValue = 1;
                            defaultEng = 'so360';
                            searchData.set('defaultEng', 'so360');
                            LogHub.behavior('somultiswitch', 'so360');

                            qboot.cookie.set(COOKIE_KEY, cookieValue, {expires: 30 * 24 * 3600 * 1000}); // 1 month
                        }
                    }());

                    if(defaultEng != 'somulti'){
                        var defaultEngData = HAO_DATA.searchTabData.searchEngConf.webpage[defaultEng];
                        if(defaultEngData){
                            g('eng-logo').className = defaultEng;
                            g('search-btn').innerHTML = defaultEngData[5] || defaultEngData[2] + '搜索';
                            g('search-kw').setAttribute('name', defaultEngData[1]);
                            g('search-form').setAttribute('action', defaultEngData[0]);

                            var defaultParamsEl = g('search-form').getElementsByTagName('div')[0],
                                paramsEl = document.createElement('div'),
                                paramsData = defaultEngData[4].split(';'),
                                paramsHtml = '';
                            paramsEl.className = 'others-params webpage-' + defaultEng + ' types-webpage';
                            while(paramsData.length){
                                var p = paramsData[0].split(':');
                                paramsHtml += '<input type="hidden" name="' + p[0] + '" value="' + p[1] + '">';
                                paramsData.shift();
                            }
                            paramsEl.innerHTML = paramsHtml;
                            g('search-form').insertBefore(paramsEl, defaultParamsEl);
                            g('search-form').removeChild(defaultParamsEl);
                        }
                    }else{
                        g('search-hsid').setAttribute('value', qboot.cookie.get('__hsid'));
                    }

                })();
            </script>

    (function () {
        var fsLiquidateApi = hao360.isHttps() ? 'https://behavior.ssl.dhrest.com/hao360cn/hotsite1' : 'http://behavior.dhrest.com/hao360cn/hotsite1',
            fsRecommendApi = hao360.isHttps() ? 'https://show-g.mediav.com/s' : 'http://show.g.mediav.com/s';

        var fsModule = (function () {
            var urlStore = (function () {
                var url = 'http://www.2345.com/360baidu1/index.htm';
                return {
                    set: function (value) {
                        url = value || url;
                    },
                    get: function () {
                        return url;
                    }
                }
            })();

            var adtracker = (function () {
                var defaultOptions = {};
                return {
                    init: function (options) {
                        defaultOptions = qboot.mix(defaultOptions, options, true);
                    },
                    pv: function () {
                        var imptk = defaultOptions.imptk,
                            imparg = defaultOptions.imparg,
                            impurl = defaultOptions.impurl;
                        while (imptk && imptk.length) {
                            logPureSender(imptk.shift());
                        }
                        if (impurl + imparg) {
                            logPureSender(impurl + imparg);
                        }
                    },
                    click: function () {
                        var clktk = defaultOptions.clktk;
                        if (clktk && clktk.length) {
                            clktk.forEach(function (item) {
                                logPureSender(item);
                            });
                        }
                    }
                }
            })();


            var addEvent = function (obj, evt, fn) {
                if (obj) {
                    (typeof window.addEventListener === 'function') ? obj.addEventListener(evt, fn, false) : obj.attachEvent('on' + evt, fn);
                }
            };

            var bindEvent = function () {
                addEvent(hao360.g("famoussite-baidu"), 'click', function (event) {
                    event.preventDefault && event.preventDefault();
                    window.open(urlStore.get());
                    return false;
                });
            };

            var loadLiquidateData = function (callback) {
                qboot.jsonp(fsLiquidateApi, {
                        fmt: 'jsonp',
                        huid: qboot.cookie.get('__huid')
                    }, function (res) {
                        if (res && res.errno == 0) {
                            callback && callback(res.data);
                        }
                    },
                    {
                        jsonp: '_callback'
                    });
            };

            var formatRecommendData = function (key, data) {
                try {
                    var ret = data['adspaces'][key]['ads'][0];
                    return {
                        impurl: data['impurl'],
                        text: ret.desc,
                        url: ret.curl,
                        imparg: ret.imparg,
                        imptk: ret.imptk,
                        clktk: ret.clktk
                    };
                }
                catch (e) {
                    return null;
                }
            };

            var loadRecommendData = function (callback) {
                var showids = '1QrGjU';
                qboot.jsonp(fsRecommendApi, {
                    type: 1,
                    of: 4,
                    newf: 2,
                    showids: showids
                }, function (res) {
                    var recData = formatRecommendData(showids, res);
                    if (recData) {
                        callback && callback(recData);
                    }
                }, {
                    jsonp: 'jsonp'
                });
            };

                    container = element.parentNode;

                    adtracker.click();
                    LogHub.behavior('famoussite-pmp', 'click');
                });
            };

        function report(project, data) {
            var HAO_MONITOR_HOST = STATIC_CONFIG.monitor.haoMonitor;
            var mix = qboot.mix,
                encodeURIJson = qboot.encodeURIJson;
            var monitorMap = {
                'hao360': 1,
                'hao360i': 8
            };

            if (monitorMap[project]) {
                var logData = mix({
                    cc: ObjectH.values(hao360.area.get()).join(),
                    appid: monitorMap[project]
                }, data, true);

                var url = HAO_MONITOR_HOST + 'stat.gif';

                var logUrl = url + '?' + encodeURIJson(logData);
                logSender(logUrl);
            }
        }

        function routine() {
            var PAGE_LOADED_TIME = (new Date).getTime();
            report('hao360i', {
                ht: HEAD_END_TIME - PAGE_START_TIME,
                rt: PAGE_READY_TIME - PAGE_START_TIME,
                lt: UNFOLD_TIME - PAGE_START_TIME,
                et: PAGE_LOADED_TIME - PAGE_START_TIME,

            });

    (function(){
        var clientWidth = window.screen.width;
        if(!clientWidth){
            return;
        }
        if(clientWidth >= 1920){
            clientWidth = 1920;
        }else if(clientWidth >= 1600){
            clientWidth = 1600;
        }else if(clientWidth >= 1440){
            clientWidth = 1440;
        }else if(clientWidth >= 1371){
            clientWidth = 1371;
        }else if(clientWidth >= 1366){
            clientWidth = 1366;
        }else if(clientWidth >= 1360){
            clientWidth = 1360;
        }else if(clientWidth >= 1300){
            clientWidth = 1300;
        }else if (clientWidth >= 1280){
            clientWidth = 1280;
        }else if(clientWidth >= 1200){
            clientWidth = 1200;
        }else if(clientWidth >= 1025){
            clientWidth = 1025;
        }else if (clientWidth >= 1024){
            clientWidth = 1024;
        }else{
            clientWidth = 800;
        }
        LogHub.behavior('screen', clientWidth);

        var clientWidth = window.screen.width;
        var docWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        if(clientWidth - docWidth > 100){
            LogHub.behavior('screen', 'different');
        }
        var changeScreen = false;
        W(document).receive("page-size-changed",function(e){
            var docWidth2 = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
            if(docWidth2 != docWidth && !changeScreen){
                LogHub.behavior('screen', 'change');
                changeScreen = true;
                setTimeout(function(){
                    LogHub.behavior('screen', docWidth2 - docWidth);

                }, 100)
            }
        });
    })();
